While you may not have an inflated sense of self-importance, your lack of emotional investment in others and your tendency to prioritize your own interests above all else set you apart from more empathetic and socially aware individuals. Your low levels of Machiavellianism and Narcissism mean you may not have a strong desire for power or admiration, but your ability to adapt and manipulate situations to your advantage remains a potent tool in your arsenal. Overall, you are a master of subtle manipulation, using your intelligence and charm to influence those around you and achieve your objectives.
